Mr. President, I rise today to recognize the 75th anniversary of the Detroit Windsor Tunnel. Detroit is Canada and the last city in the United States to have this long and successful in- year transportation project completed. The Windsor tunnel is the only in-town tunnel in the country and is the only tunnel in the entire United States that runs through Windsor, Canada.  On May 6, 1917, Detroit began construction on the northern terminus of the Detroit River. Over the next 2 years, over a thousand men and women went into work, constructing the tunnel, much of it under bridges and overpasses, to accommodate the rapid growth of Detroit.
